Capitalized terms used but not defined in this Agreement shall have the meanings set forth in the Stock Purchase Agreement, dated as of August , 2010 (the " _Stock Purchase Agreement_ "), by and among the Buyer, the Seller and the Company, a copy of which has been delivered to the Escrow Agent. W I T N E S S E T H: **WHEREAS,** the Buyer, the Seller and the Company have entered into the Stock Purchase Agreement; **WHEREAS,** the Buyer has agreed that at the Closing, pursuant to and subject to the terms and conditions set forth in the Stock Purchase Agreement, the Buyer shall deposit with the Escrow Agent the Escrow Deposit equal to Twenty-Two Million Nine Hundred Thousand Dollars ($22,900,000); and **WHEREAS,** the Escrow Agent is willing to act as escrow agent on the terms and conditions hereinafter set forth. **NOW, THEREFORE,** in consideration of the mutual covenants, agreements and conditions set forth herein, and intending to be legally bound, the parties agree as follows: 1. _Establishment of Escrow; Investments_. (a) At Closing, the Buyer shall deposit the Escrow Deposit equal to Twenty- Two Million Nine Hundred Thousand Dollars ($22,900,000) in immediately available funds with the Escrow Agent, pursuant to _Section 1.03_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement. (b) The escrowed funds (the " _Escrowed Funds_ ") shall consist of the following, whether now or hereafter acquired, together, in each case, with the proceeds thereof: (A)(i) the Escrow Deposit; plus (ii) the investments in which the Escrow Agent may invest such amount hereunder; plus (iii) interest, dividends and other income, if any, resulting from the investment of such amounts and earnings thereon; _less_ (B) in each case, any amounts actually distributed to the Buyer or the Seller pursuant to this Agreement and the Stock Purchase Agreement and any amount actually withdrawn by the Escrow Agent hereunder. (c) The Escrow Agent shall retain the Escrowed Funds in a separate account called the Project Green Acres Escrow subject to the terms and conditions hereof and is empowered and directed to invest and reinvest all of the Escrowed Funds only in such specific investments as are set forth herein or as the Buyer and the Seller shall from time to time jointly direct in writing to the Escrow Agent. Any other investments shall be limited to: (i) time and demand deposits, certificates of deposit and acceptances, maturing within thirty (30) days from the date of acquisition thereof, issued by state and national banks located in the United States of America, including the Escrow Agent or any of its affiliates, and having capital, surplus and profits aggregating at least One Hundred Million Dollars ($100,000,000); (ii) securities or other obligations of, or guaranteed by, the United States of America or any agency thereof maturing within thirty (30) days from the acquisition thereof; (iii) commercial paper, maturing within thirty (30) days from the date of acquisition thereof, rated A-1 or P-1 by Standard and Poors or Moodys Investors Service; (iv) repurchase agreements fully collateralized by obligations described in Sections 1(c)(i), 1(c)(ii) or 1(c)(iii) hereof; or (v) shares of investment companies registered under the Investment Company Act of 1940 which invest in any obligation described herein, including those for which the Escrow Agent or any of its affiliates provide services for a fee, whether as an investment advisor, custodian, transfer agent, registrar, sponsor, distributor, manager or otherwise. (d) The Escrow Agent is further authorized to sell or redeem any or all paid investments without further instructions as may be necessary from time to time to pay in cash any amount required to be paid pursuant to this Agreement. (e) Unless otherwise directed in writing by the Buyer and the Seller, the Escrow Agent shall not invest all or any portion of the Escrowed Funds in any investment if the maturity date of such investment is later than the date thirty (30) days from the date of acquisition thereof. (f) In the absence of written instructions pursuant to Section 1(c) of this Agreement, the Escrow Agent shall invest the Escrowed Funds in the [ ] or such other money market funds customarily utilized by the Escrow Agents corporate trust department in the ordinary course of business of its corporate trust business in the usual performance of its escrow agent duties. 2. _Purpose of Escrowed Funds_. The purpose of the Escrowed Funds is to, subject to the terms and conditions of the Stock Purchase Agreement, secure (i) any post-Closing reduction in the Purchase Price pursuant to _Section 1.05_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement (a " _Post-Closing Adjustment_ ") and (ii) the indemnification obligations set forth in _Section 9.01_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement. 3. _Post-Closing Adjustment_. If the Purchase Price is adjusted downward as a result of the final determination of the Closing Net Working Capital in accordance with _Section 1.05_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement, then within five (5) Business Days of the date on which the Closing Net Working Capital is finally determined pursuant to _Section 1.05_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement, the Buyer and the Seller shall deliver joint written instructions to the Escrow Agent specifying the dollar amount of such downward adjustment pursuant to _Section 1.05_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement and instructing the Escrow Agent to release such amount to the Buyer. Promptly after receipt of such notice (and in no event more than five (5) Business Days thereafter), the Escrow Agent shall release to the Buyer from the Escrowed Funds an amount equal to such specified dollar amount. 4. _Indemnification Claims_. The Buyer shall be entitled to make indemnification claims (the " _Indemnification Claims_ ") against the Escrowed Funds for Losses incurred by the Buyer or the Buyer Indemnified Parties in accordance with the procedures set forth in _Article IX_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement (subject to the limitations and requirements set forth in the Stock Purchase Agreement and this Section 4). Any Indemnification Claim by the Buyer against the Escrowed Funds shall be presented to the Escrow Agent and the Seller as follows: (a) Indemnification Claims against the Escrowed Funds may be made only by the Buyer, on its own behalf or on behalf of any other Buyer Indemnified Party. The Buyer shall provide the Escrow Agent and the Seller with a written notice, pursuant to _Article IX_ of the Stock Purchase Agreement, setting forth: (i) that the Indemnified Party has actually incurred Losses in an aggregate stated amount; and (ii) a brief description, in reasonable detail (to the extent reasonably available to the Indemnified Party), of the facts, circumstances or events giving rise to the Losses actually incurred by the Indemnified Party, the amount of Losses actually incurred by the Indemnified Party, the date each such item was incurred, and the specific nature of the breach of the Stock Purchase Agreement to which such item is related. In the case of a Third Party Claim, the Buyer shall also provide the identity and address of the third-party claimant (to the extent reasonably available to the Indemnified Party) and copies of any formal demand or complaint. (b) The Escrow Agent shall not release any amounts from the Escrowed Funds in respect of any Indemnification Claim unless and until the validity of such Indemnification Claim is finally resolved, either by mutual agreement of the Buyer and the Seller or by a court of competent jurisdiction, and the Escrow Agent receives joint written notice of such resolution from the Buyer and the Seller stating the amount, if any, that any Indemnified Party is entitled to receive with respect to such Indemnification Claim (a " _Resolved Claim Notice_ "). Within five (5) Business Days after the receipt of a Resolved Claim Notice that provides for the payment of any amount to the Buyer or any other Buyer Indemnified Party, the Escrow Agent shall deliver to such Person an amount equal to the amount set forth in the Resolved Claim Notice. 5. _Amounts Earned on Escrow; Tax Matters_. The Parties agree that, for all income tax purposes, the Escrowed Funds shall be treated as owned by the Seller unless and until released to the Buyer pursuant to Sections 3 or 4 of this Agreement, so that all interest or other income earned from the investment of the Escrowed Funds shall be considered to be income of the Seller. The release of any portion of the Escrowed Funds to the Seller shall be treated as additional consideration paid, on the date of the release from the Escrowed Funds, on behalf of the Buyer pursuant to the Stock Purchase Agreement, except to the extent that any amount so released to the Seller is required to be treated as interest pursuant to Section 1272 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended. Pursuant to the terms of the Patriot Act and the Escrow Agents internal policies, all signatories to agreements with the Escrow Agent must provide their tax identification numbers on IRS Form W-9. In addition, the Escrow Agents sales staff must run Dun and Bradstreet reports on all corporate signatories (which incorporates an Office of Foreign Assets Control check) and secure personal, photo identification from individuals (passports, drivers license, etc). In the absence of Dun and Bradstreet reports, articles of association, good standing certificates and other documentation reasonably requested by the Escrow Agent shall be delivered by the other parties hereto. All such Patriot Act documentation must be furnished to the Escrow Agent prior to the execution of this Escrow Agreement. The Escrow Agent shall issue an IRS Form 1099 (or any successor form) relating to such taxable income or gains to and in the name of the Seller with respect to all earnings on the Escrowed Funds, and shall issue such other information returns as required by law with respect to the disbursement of the Escrowed Funds. At the request of the Seller from time to time, the Buyer and the Seller shall deliver joint written instructions to the Escrow Agent to release from the Escrowed Funds an amount equal to any tax payable by the Seller with respect to interest or other income earned from the investment of the Escrowed Funds. 6. _Release of Escrowed Funds_. (a) The date that is twelve (12) months after the Closing Date is the " _Release Date_." On the first Business Day after the Release Date, the Escrow Agent shall disburse the Available Escrow Amount to the Seller. The " _Available Escrow Amount_ " means all of the Escrowed Funds on such date, less any amount that is subject to any pending Indemnification Claim made by the Buyer prior to the Release Date which has not been resolved as of the Release Date. (b) Any amount of the Escrowed Funds retained after the Release Date in respect of any pending Indemnification Claim shall not be subject to or retained in respect of any other Indemnification Claim after such date and shall be released (in whole or in part) by the Escrow Agent to the Buyer or the Seller (as the case may be) upon the receipt by the Escrow Agent of either: (i) a copy of a written settlement agreement executed by the Buyer and the Seller resolving such pending Indemnification Claim with joint instructions of the Buyer and the Seller that all or part of the Escrowed Funds be released to the Buyer and/or the Seller; or (ii) a copy of a final order or judgment by a court of competent jurisdiction instructing the Escrow Agent to release all or part of the Escrowed Funds to the Buyer and/or the Seller. If some but not all of the Escrowed Funds are released, the Escrow Agent shall continue to hold the remaining part of the Escrowed Funds until such time as it receives further joint instructions or a final order or judgment, as described in this Section 6. (c) In addition to, and without limitation of the foregoing provisions of this Section 6, the Escrow Agent shall make distributions from the Escrowed Funds any time and from time to time upon, and in accordance with, joint written instructions from the Buyer and the Seller. 7. _Termination_. Unless terminated earlier with the joint written consent of the Buyer and the Seller, this Agreement shall remain in full force and effect until all of the Escrowed Funds shall have been released in accordance with the terms hereof. 8. _The Escrow Agent_. (a) The Buyer and the Seller hereby appoint the Escrow Agent to act as escrow agent and to hold the Escrowed Funds, and the Escrow Agent hereby accepts such appointment, upon the terms and conditions set forth herein. (b) The Buyer shall pay the Escrow Agents costs and fees for its ordinary services under this Agreement. The Escrow Agent shall be entitled to an administrative fee of $[ ] per year for the services to be rendered by it hereunder and to be reimbursed for all losses, liabilities or reasonable out-of-pocket expenses, including reasonable attorneys fees, incurred or made by it without gross negligence, bad faith or willful misconduct arising out of or in connection with its entering into this Agreement or carrying out its duties hereunder, including the costs and expenses of defending itself against any claim of liability with respect to this Agreement. Any such compensation and reimbursement to which the Escrow Agent is entitled shall be borne 50% by the Buyer and 50% by the Seller. (c) The duties and responsibilities of the Escrow Agent hereunder shall be determined solely by the express provisions of this Agreement. The Escrow Agent undertakes to perform only such duties as are expressly set forth herein and no further duties or responsibilities shall be implied. The Escrow Agent shall not in any way be bound or affected by a notice or modification or cancellation of this Agreement, unless written notice thereof is given to the Escrow Agent by the Buyer and the Seller. (d) In performing any duties under this Agreement, the Escrow Agent shall not be liable for damages, losses, or expenses, except for gross negligence, willful misconduct or bad faith on the part of the Escrow Agent. The Escrow Agent shall not incur any such liability for (i) any act or failure to act made or omitted in good faith, or (ii) any action taken or omitted in reliance upon any instrument, including any written statement or affidavit provided for in this Agreement, that such agent shall in good faith believe to be genuine, nor will the Escrow Agent be liable or responsible for forgeries, fraud, impersonations, or determining the scope of any representative authority. The Escrow Agent is not responsible for determining and verifying the authority of any such person acting or purporting to act on behalf of any other party to this Agreement. (e) If any controversy arises between the parties to this Agreement, or with any other party, concerning the subject matter of this Agreement, its terms or conditions, the Escrow Agent will not be required to determine the controversy or to take any action regarding it. The Escrow Agent may hold the Escrowed Funds and may wait for settlement of any such controversy by final appropriate legal proceedings or other means as, in the Escrow Agents discretion, may be required, despite what may be set forth elsewhere in this Agreement. In such event, the Escrow Agent will not be liable for interest or damage. Furthermore, the Escrow Agent may at its option, file an action of interpleader requiring the parties to answer and litigate any claims and rights among themselves. The Escrow Agent is authorized to deposit with the clerk of the court the entire Escrowed Funds. Upon initiating such action, the Escrow Agent shall be fully released and discharged of and from all obligations and liabilities imposed by the terms of this Agreement, except for obligations or liabilities arising by reason of the prior negligence, willful misconduct or bad faith on the part of the Escrow Agent. (f) The Escrow Agent agrees that the Buyer and the Seller may, by mutual agreement at any time, remove it as Escrow Agent hereunder and substitute an individual or a bank or trust company for it, in which event the Escrow Agent, upon receipt of written notice thereof, shall account for and deliver to such substituted escrow agent all funds and obligations held by it, less any amounts then due and unpaid to it for fees and expenses as herein provided, and the Escrow Agent shall thereafter be discharged from all liability hereunder for events arising after such removal. (g) The Escrow Agent may at any time resign as such by delivering written notice of resignation to the other parties hereto. If the Buyer and the Seller jointly designate a successor escrow agent, then the Escrow Agent shall deliver the Escrowed Funds to such successor escrow agent, whereupon the Escrow Agent shall be discharged of any liability or responsibility with respect thereto arising thereafter. If, within thirty (30) days after receipt of such notice of resignation, the Buyer and the Seller have not jointly designated a successor escrow agent, the Escrow Agent may deposit the Escrowed Funds into a court of competent jurisdiction in the State of [ ], and upon such deposit, the Escrow Agent shall be relieved of any liability or responsibility with respect thereto arising thereafter. Any corporation or association into which the Escrow Agent in its individual capacity may be merged or converted or with which it may be consolidated, or any corporation or association resulting from any merger, conversion or consolidation to which the Escrow Agent in its individual capacity shall be a party, or any corporation or association to which all or substantially all the corporate trust business of the Escrow Agent in its individual capacity may be sold or otherwise transferred, shall be the Escrow Agent hereunder without further action of the Buyer or the Seller hereunder. 9. _Governing Law_. The Parties agree that all terms and conditions of this Agreement shall be governed by and construed and enforced in accordance with the laws of the State of [ ] without giving effect to any choice of law or conflict of laws provision or rule that would cause the application of the laws of any jurisdiction other than the State of [ ]. 10. _Notices_. All notices and other communications hereunder shall be in writing and shall be deemed given on the same day if delivered personally, or by facsimile transmission with voice confirmation of receipt, or shall be deemed given on the date receipt is confirmed if mailed by registered or certified mail or commercial overnight courier (e.g., UPS, Federal Express, Network Courier, Sonic, etc.), return receipt or confirmation of delivery requested, to the Escrow Agent at: [ ] [ ] [ ] Attention: [ ] Telephone: [ ] Facsimile: [ ] and to the other parties hereto at the addresses set forth in the Stock Purchase Agreement (or, in any case, at such other address for a party as shall be specified by like notice). 11. _Effect on Successors in Interest, Assignees_. This Agreement shall inure to the benefit of and be binding upon the heirs, administrators, executors, assignees and successors of each of the parties hereto. Except as provided herein, the rights and obligations of the parties hereto under this Agreement shall not be assigned to any other person or entity without the prior written consent of the other parties hereto not to be unreasonably withheld. 12. _Service of Process; Jurisdiction_. The parties hereto agree that any action concerning any and all claims, disputes or controversies arising out of or relating to this Agreement shall only be commenced in the State of [ ]. The parties hereto further agree to accept service of any pleadings (and such service shall be valid, to the full extent permissible under the laws of the State of [ ]), if made to the respective parties at the addresses and in the manner set forth in Section 10 of this Agreement. 13. _Additional Agreements_. The parties hereto agree to execute and deliver any and all documents and to take such further action as shall be reasonably required to effectuate the provisions of this Agreement. 14. _Entire Agreement; Amendment_. This Agreement, including all exhibits and schedules hereto, contains the entire understanding of the Escrow Agent and the other parties hereto with respect to the subject matter contained herein and supersedes all prior agreements and understandings between the Escrow Agent and the other parties hereto related to the subject matter hereof. This Agreement and the Stock Purchase Agreement, including all exhibits and schedules hereto and thereto, contain the entire understanding of the Buyer and the Seller with respect to the subject matter contained herein and therein and supersede all prior agreements and understandings between them related to the subject matter hereof and thereof. No modification or amendment of or with respect to any provisions of this Escrow Agreement shall be effective unless it shall be in writing and signed by the Buyer, the Seller and the Escrow Agent and shall designate specifically the terms and provisions so modified. 15. _Inconsistencies_. In the event that any claim of inconsistency arises between this Agreement and the terms of the Stock Purchase Agreement, as they may from time to time be amended, the terms of the Stock Purchase Agreement shall control, except with respect to the duties, liabilities and rights, including compensation and indemnification, of the Escrow Agent as escrow agent, which shall be controlled by the terms of this Agreement. 16. _Counterparts_. This Agreement may be executed in counterparts, each of which shall be deemed an original, and all of which together shall constitute one and the same instrument. _[Signature Page Follows]_ IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the parties have executed this Escrow Agreement as of the date first written above. | **BUYER** ---|--- | | [ ] | | | By: | | Name: | Title: | ** ** | ** ** | **SELLER** | | [ ] | | | By: | | Name: | Title: | ** ** | ** ** | **ESCROW AGENT** | | [ ] | | | By: | | Name: | Title: _[Signature Page to Escrow Agreement]_ ** _EXHIBIT G_** **Transfer of Non-Company Employees and Non-U.S. Employees** G.1. For a period of one (1) year after the Closing, at the cost and expense of the Buyer or an Affiliate, the Buyer or its Affiliates will maintain the current locations of a majority of the Field Offices of the Seller and its Subsidiaries as of the Closing Date and will continue to use each such Field Office as the place of employment of the Non-Company Employees who were based at such Field Office as of the Closing and who continue to be employed by, or accept offers of employment with, the Buyer of an Affiliate. For a period of one (1) year after the Closing, the Buyer and its Affiliates shall not move any Field Office if such a move would reasonably be expected to disrupt the commutes of the employees in such Field Office. G.2. The Seller and the Buyer will cooperate with each other in contacting Non-Company Employees regarding offers of employment by the Buyer or its Affiliates, subject to Applicable Law, as soon as reasonably practicable after the signing of this Agreement. The Seller and the Buyer will arrange for senior managers of each Party to conduct joint visits to each applicable Seller or Company location and make joint presentations to Non-Company Employees regarding the strategic benefits of the Transactions and the benefits to Non-Company Employees of accepting such offers of employment. G.3. Except for Non-Company Employees located in jurisdictions in which the employment of the Non-Company Employees continues automatically as a result of "transfer of undertaking" or similar foreign laws, the Buyer or its Affiliates shall make a "qualified offer" to each of the Non-Company Employees. For any such employees who receive a "qualified offer" from the Buyer or its Affiliates, the Seller shall notify such employees that if the employees decline to accept such offer, the Seller or its Subsidiary, as applicable, will terminate such employees and will not rehire such employees, and the Seller or its Subsidiary shall offer such employees the severance payment to which they are entitled from the Seller or its Subsidiary. For the avoidance of doubt, in the event of a dispute regarding the amount of such severance, the Seller or its Subsidiary may settle such dispute in its discretion. A "qualified offer" means salary and bonus or similar incentive compensation equivalent to or better than the salary and bonus or similar incentive compensation the employee currently has and other benefits (including participation in equity incentive plans) that are no less favorable in the aggregate for such employee than those provided to a comparable employee of the Buyer or its Affiliates in the applicable jurisdiction. G.4. For the period from the Closing Date through the first (1st) anniversary thereof, the Buyer or its Affiliate shall provide each Non-Company Employee referred to in Section G.3 with (i) compensation (including salary, wages and historical bonus potential but excluding any equity-based compensation, transaction, severance or change of control bonuses or payments) that is no less favorable in the aggregate than the compensation provided by the Seller or its Subsidiary immediately prior to the Closing, and (ii) employee benefits plans, programs and arrangements that in all material respects are no less favorable in the aggregate than the employee benefits as in effect for other employees of the Buyer or its Affiliate in the applicable countries immediately prior to the Closing. G.5. For Non-Company Employees located in jurisdictions in which the employment of the Non-Company Employees continues automatically as a result of "transfer of undertaking" or similar foreign laws, the Buyer or its Affiliate, as applicable, shall continue such employees employment in accordance with Applicable Laws. G.6. For a period of two (2) years after the Closing Date, the Seller shall not, directly or indirectly, solicit or rehire any Non-Company Employee who is offered employment by the Buyer or its Affiliates, whether such Non- Company Employee accepts or declines such offer of employment. Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Seller shall have the right to employ any Non-Company Employee who is not offered employment by the Buyer or its Affiliates. G.7. If the employment of any Non-U.S. Employee listed on _Schedule G.6_ of the Company Disclosure Schedules to whom the Buyer or an Affiliate does not wish to offer employment otherwise would continue after the Closing as a result of "transfer of undertaking" or similar foreign laws, the Seller shall use reasonable efforts prior to the Closing to negotiate a separation arrangement with such Non-U.S. Employee and shall be responsible for any separation payment to such Non-U.S. Employee. If the Seller is unable to negotiate such an arrangement and the employment of such Non-U.S. Employee is continued with the Buyer or an Affiliate after the Closing as a result of such laws, the Seller will be responsible for reimbursing the Buyer or such Affiliate for fifty percent (50%) of the compensation paid by the Buyer or such Affiliate to such Non-U.S. Employee for up to six (6) months after the Closing and for reimbursing the Buyer or such Affiliate for any mandatory severance (up to the amount that would have been payable if the Seller had severed such Non-U.S. Employee as of the Closing) if the Buyer or such Affiliate terminates such Non-U.S. Employee during such six (6) month period. G.8. The Seller represents that no employees of the Seller (other than the employees specified on Schedule G.6 of the Company Disclosure Schedules) will ever assert that they dedicated greater than 50% of their time to the metrology business of the Company and consequently are entitled to be employed by the Buyer. In the event any such employee makes any such claim, the Seller shall indemnify the Buyer for any Losses arising from such claim. G.9. The Buyer shall indemnify the Seller and its Affiliates for any severance payments or similar costs relating to the Non-Company Employees incurred by the Seller or its Affiliates arising from any actions or inactions of the Buyer or its Affiliates after the Closing, except for the costs agreed to be borne by the Seller in Section G.6. The Seller shall indemnify the Buyer and its Affiliates for any severance payments or similar costs relating to the Non-Company Employees incurred by the Buyer or its Affiliates arising from any actions or inactions of the Seller or its Affiliates before the Closing, except for the costs agreed to be borne by the Buyer under this Agreement. G.10. At any time prior to the Closing, the Seller may transfer, or cause to be transferred, to the Company any Non-Company Employees; _provided_ , _however_ , that the Seller shall not increase the compensation or benefits of such employees in connection with such transfer, except in the Ordinary Course of Business. G.11. The Seller shall pay (i) the bonus compensation and profit sharing liabilities set forth on Schedule 5.08 of the Company Disclosure Schedules (which amounts shall be prorated for the partial year ended on the Closing Date and shall expressly exclude any accrued sales commissions) within thirty (30) days after the Closing and (ii) the transaction incentive payments and severance payments set forth on Schedule 5.08 of the Company Disclosure Schedules within thirty (30) days after the Closing or at such later date as is contemplated by the applicable agreement governing any such payments. G.12. With respect to each benefit plan, program, practice, policy or arrangement (including the severance plans, policies, or arrangements, and paid time off, vacation, and sick leave policies of the Transferee or its Affiliates) maintained by the Transferee or its Affiliates and in which any of the Non-U.S. Transferred Employees become eligible to participate (the " _Transferee Plans_ "), for purposes of determining eligibility to participate, vesting and benefit accrual, employment service with the applicable Transferor (or predecessor employers to the extent the applicable Transferor provides past service credit) shall be treated as employment service with the Transferee and/or any of its applicable Affiliates; _provided_ , _however_ , that such prior employment service shall not be recognized to the extent that such recognition would result in a duplication of benefits. Such credit for prior employment service also shall apply for purposes of satisfying any waiting periods or evidence of insurability requirements applicable under any of the Transferee Plans. To the extent applicable, the Transferee or its Affiliate shall use its commercially reasonable efforts to cause each of the applicable Transferee Plans to (i) waive all limitations as to pre-existing condition exclusions, evidence of insurability requirements and waiting periods with respect to participation and coverage requirements applicable to Non-U.S. Transferred Employees and their eligible dependents under the Transferee Plans, except to the extent that such limitations, evidence of insurability and waiting periods were applicable to such individuals under a comparable benefit plan of the applicable Transferor, and (ii) give Non-U.S. Transferred Employees and their eligible dependents credit under the Transferee Plans for amounts paid during the year in which the Closing occurs under a corresponding benefit plan of the applicable Transferor for purposes of satisfying any applicable deductibles, co-payments and out-of-pocket maximums as though such amounts had been paid in accordance with the terms and conditions of the Transferee Plans. G.13. The Transferee or its Affiliate shall honor all balances under the vacation, paid time off and sick leave policies of the applicable Transferor accrued by Non-U.S. Transferred Employees to the extent set forth in the Statement of Closing Net Working Capital as finally determined in accordance with Section 1.05 of the Agreement; provided, however, that the Transferee or its Affiliate shall not be required to honor such balances for a Non-U.S. Employee to the extent that (i) the applicable Transferor or any Affiliate is required by Applicable Law to pay off the cash value of such balances of such Non-U.S. Transferred Employee in connection with the consummation of the Transactions, or (ii) any such balance (on a per employee basis) exceeds the sum of two (2) weeks and the aggregate number of 2010 annual vacation, paid time off and sick leave days accrued for the account of such Non-U.S. Transferred Employee as of the Closing Date. All such balances that are not required to be honored by the Transferee or its Affiliate pursuant to the limitations described in clauses (i) and (ii) above shall be paid by the Seller or a Subsidiary of the Seller (other than the Company) at or promptly following the Closing, except as otherwise required by Applicable Law. G.14. The parties shall (or shall cause their respective Affiliates to) take all steps, as soon as possible, as are required under Applicable Law and/or any applicable collective bargaining, works council or similar agreement, to notify, consult with, or negotiate the effect, impact, terms or timing of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement with each works council, trade union, employee representative group or Governmental Body as early as possible after the signing of this Agreement. G.15. Nothing contained in the Agreement, including this Exhibit G, expressed or implied, is intended to confer upon any Non-U.S. Employee any benefits under any employee benefit plan, fund or program, including severance benefits or the right to employment or continued employment with the Buyer, the Transferee or any Affiliate for any period by reason of this Agreement. In addition, the provisions of the Agreement, in particular this Exhibit G, are for the sole benefit of the parties hereto and their respective Affiliates and are not for the benefit of any third parties. G.16. The Buyer and the Seller shall, and shall cause their respective Affiliates to, use reasonable efforts to effect the transfer of the Non-U.S. Transferred Employees from each Transferor to the Transferee or its Affiliates in accordance with Applicable Law. A Transferor may terminate the employment of any Non-U.S. Employee who does not become a Non-U.S. Transferred Employee on the Closing Date. The Buyer and the Seller shall, and shall cause their respective Affiliates to, use reasonable efforts to eliminate or minimize any Losses incurred (including, for the avoidance of doubt, any severance or other termination-related payments made) by any party (i) in connection with the transfer of the Non-U.S. Transferred Employees to the Transferee or an Affiliate hereunder, (ii) in connection with the termination or any deemed termination of a Non-U.S. Employee, or (iii) arising or in connection with a refusal of any Non-U.S. Employee to become a Non-U.S. Transferred Employee. ** _EXHIBIT H_** **Consulting Agreement Terms** If Mark Munch and the Buyer do not enter into a mutually satisfactory employment agreement, then a transition consulting agreement, between the Buyer and Mark Munch (the " _Munch Agreement_ "), on the following material terms and conditions will be deemed satisfactory to Buyer: 1. The term of engagement shall be equal to or greater than six (6) months. 2. Mr. Munch shall provide full-time consulting services for the metrology business of the Company. 3. During the term of Mr. Munchs engagement, the Buyer shall provide compensation at least equivalent to Mr. Munchs current salary. 4. The Munch Agreement shall contain customary assignment of inventions and confidentiality provisions used by the Buyer for consultants, and a one-year restriction after the termination of such consulting upon soliciting or hiring employees of the Buyer; provided, however that the Munch Agreement shall not include any language that would restrict or limit Mr. Munchs ability to work for, invest in or provide services to, any other Person following the termination or expiration of his engagement with the Buyer. Except as otherwise forth above, the Munch Agreement shall not contain any additional terms or conditions that could reasonably be deemed material and adverse to Mr. Munch. ** _EXHIBIT I_** **Form of Transition Services Agreement** **THIS** **TRANSITION SERVICES AGREEMENT** (this " _Agreement_ ") is entered into as of , 2010 (the " _Effective Date_ "), by and between [ ], a Delaware corporation (the " _Seller_ "), and [ ], an Arizona corporation (the " _Company_ "). The Seller and the Company are sometimes referred to herein as a " _Party_ " and collectively as the " _Parties_." Capitalized terms used herein and not otherwise defined herein shall have the meanings given to such terms in the Purchase Agreement (defined below). _RECITALS_ WHEREAS, pursuant to that certain Stock Purchase Agreement, dated , 2010 (the " _Purchase Agreement_ "), by and among the Seller, the Company and [ ], a [ ] (the " _Buyer_ "), (i) the Buyer has agreed to purchase from the Seller, and the Seller has agreed to sell to the Buyer, all of the capital stock of the Company, and (ii) the Buyer, through itself or one or more of its direct or indirect Subsidiaries, has agreed to purchase and assume from the Seller or one or more of its direct or indirect Subsidiaries, and the Seller, through itself or one or more of its direct or indirect Subsidiaries, has agreed to sell, transfer and assign to the Buyer or one of more of its Subsidiaries, certain assets and liabilities described in the Purchase Agreement; WHEREAS, the Company is interested in obtaining certain transition services from the Seller following the Closing Date, subject to the terms and conditions contained herein; and WHEREAS, the Seller desires to provide the Company with certain transition services following the Closing Date, subject to the terms and conditions contained herein. NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the promises and covenants set forth herein, the Seller and the Company each hereby agree as follows: _AGREEMENT_ 1. _Transition Services_. Subject to the terms and conditions herein, the Seller shall provide, or shall cause one or more of its Service Providers (defined below) to provide, to the Company the services described on _Schedule A_ attached hereto (each, a " _Transition Service_ " and collectively, the " _Transition Services_ "). For purposes of this Agreement, " _Service Providers_ " shall mean (a) any subsidiary or affiliate of the Seller, (b) any independent contractor that is providing services to the Seller on the Closing Date as identified on a list of Service Providers furnished by the Seller to the Company no later than the execution hereof, and (c) such other third parties as may from time to time be designated in writing by the Seller to the Company and accepted by the Company, which acceptance shall not be unreasonably delayed, conditioned or withheld. The Company shall have the right to contract directly with any Service Provider and terminate the work performed by such Service Provider from the scope of this Agreement pursuant to Section 3(b). The Seller shall have the right, in its sole discretion, to subcontract any or all of the work to be performed by the Seller under this Agreement. In the event of any such subcontract, the Company shall have the right to enter into an agreement directly with such proposed subcontractor. The Seller and the Company also agree to take the other transition-related actions set forth in _Schedule B_ attached hereto. 2. _Level of Transition Services_. (a) The Seller will perform the Transition Services in the manner and at a level of service, functionality and performance, with respect to any Transition Service, substantially similar to that provided by the Seller to the Company during the period immediately prior to the Closing; provided, however, in no event will the Seller be required to (i) favor the Company or the provision of the Transition Services over the Sellers other business operations, provided that the treatment of the Company by the Seller in such regard shall be consistent with that of the Seller towards the Company prior to the date hereof, (ii) purchase, lease or license any additional equipment or software in connection with the Transition Services, or (iii) pay any costs related to the transfer or conversion of data to the Company or any alternative supplier of the Transition Services. If there is an unavoidable conflict between the immediate needs of the Seller and those of the Company as to the use of or access to a particular Transition Service, the Seller will have the right, in its sole discretion, to establish reasonable priorities, at particular times and under particular circumstances, as between the Parties so long as such priorities are consistent with prior practice between the Seller and the Company in such regard prior to the date hereof and so long as the establishment of any such reasonable priorities is done in conjunction and cooperation with the Company in good faith. (b) The Parties agree that it is the intention of the Company and the Seller that the Companys use of the Transition Services shall be for substantially the same purposes as immediately prior to the Closing and shall not be materially greater than the use required by the Company immediately prior to the Closing (including as to volume, amount, level and frequency, as applicable), except for Transition Services (including, without limitation, the IP Transition Services set forth in Section III ("Information Technology Services") of _Schedule A_) that would not have been required by the Company but for the consummation of the transactions contemplated by the Purchase Agreement, which the Parties acknowledge may require more or additional resources than were previously required by the Company. (c) Neither the Company nor its subsidiaries shall resell any Transition Services to any person whatsoever or permit the use of the Transition Services by any person other than in connection with the conduct of the business of the Company or its subsidiaries. (d) The Company agrees that the Transition Services provided by the Seller or any Service Provider, and any other assets licensed or leased from third parties and used in connection with the Transition Services, remain subject to the terms and conditions of any subcontracts or other agreements between the Seller, such Service Providers or other third parties, and the Company shall adhere to such terms and conditions. (e) The parties shall cooperate with each other to provide each other such information, materials and other cooperation that in the reasonable judgment of the requesting party are necessary to enable the requesting party to perform its obligations hereunder. 3. _Term and Termination_. (a) The term of this Agreement shall commence on the Effective Date and continue with respect to each of the Transition Services for the respective terms set forth in _Schedule A_ , unless earlier terminated pursuant to Section 3(b), and the last date in each such term being referred to herein as a " _Service Termination Date_ " for each such Transition Service. (b) The Company may terminate any Transition Service by giving the Seller prior written notice of termination of the Transition Service as set forth in _Schedule A_. As soon as reasonably practical following receipt of any such notice, the Seller shall advise the Company as to whether termination of such Transition Service will (i) require the termination or partial termination of, or otherwise affect the provision of, any other Transition Services, or (ii) result in any early termination costs, including those related to third party providers. Upon such termination of any Transition Service, the Seller shall cease, and cause its Service Providers to cease, providing the terminated Transition Service; _provided_ , _however_ , that the Company shall reimburse the Seller for any reasonable out of pocket termination costs actually payable by the Seller to Service Providers resulting from the Companys early termination of such Transition Services, as long as the Seller provided the Company notice of such termination costs after the Company submitted its notice of proposed termination of the applicable Transition Service. (c) Notwithstanding the foregoing, this Agreement will terminate in its entirety upon the earliest to occur of the following dates (the " _Termination Date_ "): (i)(A) the date on which the Seller gives written notice of termination to the Company if the Company is in default of any payment obligation to the Seller hereunder or if the Company is in default of or breaches any other provision of this Agreement which default or breach is not capable of being cured within thirty (30) days after the Companys receipt of notice of such default or breach from the Seller, or (B) if the Company is in default of or breaches any other provision of this Agreement which default or breach is capable of being cured, and such default or breach has not been cured within thirty (30) days after the Companys receipt of notice of such default or breach from the Seller; or (ii) the date on which the Seller or the Company gives written notice of termination to the other Party at any time following the last of the Service Termination Dates. (d) Effective as of the Termination Date, the Seller shall cease, and cause its Service Providers to cease, providing the Transition Services. 4. _General Intent._ The Company shall use commercially reasonable efforts to reduce and discontinue its use of the Transition Services as soon as reasonably possible following the Effective Date and in all events to end use with respect to each Transition Service not later than the applicable Service Termination Date. 5. _Fees_. (a) _Consideration_. As consideration for the Transition Services, the Company will pay to the Seller (or to the Sellers Service Providers, if requested by the Seller) the amount for each Transition Service as specified in _Schedule A_ with respect to such Transition Service. The Seller and Service Providers, as applicable, shall be entitled to charge the Company for any sales tax, withholding tax, or similar charges that they are legally required to charge or withhold on such amounts. Amounts payable hereunder will be billed and paid in U.S. dollars. If there is no fee specified in _Schedule A_ for a particular Transition Service, then the Seller shall be entitled to charge the Company for (i) 100% of any out-of- pocket expenses paid by the Seller to a third party for such Transition Service and (ii) 50% of the Sellers internal cost allocable to such Transition Service, including a fair and reasonable allocation for the Sellers wage or salary and employee benefit costs relating to employees providing such Transition Service and for the Sellers facilities and other overhead. In addition to the Transition Services fees set forth herein, the Company shall also pay any amounts the Seller is required to pay to a vendor for software used by the Seller in connection with the provision of any Transition Services, and any amounts the Seller is required to pay to a vendor to obtain its consent to allow the Seller to use such software to provide the Transition Services, provided that the Seller shall consult with the Company in good faith in connection therewith and the parties shall work together in good faith to minimize any such amounts. (b) _Invoices_. Within twenty (20) days after the end of each month, the Seller will submit one (1) invoice to the Company for all fees and expenses relating to the Transition Services provided to the Company by the Seller and its Service Providers; provided, that the Seller may instruct the Company to make payments directly to one or more Service Providers. (c) _Payment Due Date_. The Company will pay all amounts due pursuant to this Agreement within thirty (30) days after the date of each invoice. Interest shall be due and payable by the Company at the rate of 1.5% per month or the maximum legal rate, whichever is lower, on any undisputed portion of an invoice which has not been paid within such thirty (30) day period. In addition to the charges for the Transition Services provided hereunder, the Company will reimburse the Service Providers (at cost) for any and all actual out-of-pocket ancillary fees, costs, or expenses incurred by the respective Service Provider in connection with providing Transition Services hereunder, including shipping and transportation costs, duties, and taxes in accordance with the applicable agreements between the Seller and such Service Providers. 6. _Personnel_. (a) _Right to Designate and Change Personnel_. The Seller will make available such personnel as will be required to provide the Transition Services. The Seller may, in its sole discretion, designate which personnel will perform the Transition Services. The Seller also may, in its sole discretion and with at least ten (10) days prior written notice to the Company if feasible, remove and replace any such personnel at any time or, subject to Section 1 hereof, designate any Service Provider at any time to perform the Transition Services; _provided_ , _however_ , that the Seller will use its commercially reasonable efforts to limit the disruption to the Company in the transition of the Transition Services to different personnel or a third party but the Seller will have no obligation to retain any individual employee for the sole purpose of providing the applicable Transition Services. Further, in providing the Transition Services, the Seller shall not be obligated to hire any additional personnel. (b) _Personnel Wages and Expenses_. The Seller and its Service Providers will pay for all personnel expenses, including wages and benefits, of their employees and agents performing the Transition Services. Any request by the Company for travel by any employee or agent of the Seller or any Service Provider will be considered additional services, and the costs and expenses relating to such travel shall be paid by the Company, provided that any such travel and related expenses shall be in accordance with the Sellers standard travel policies for its own employees or, if applicable, in accordance with the agreement between the Seller and the applicable Service Provider. (c) _Seller Manager_. The Seller will appoint an employee (the " _Seller Manager_ ") to have overall responsibility for coordinating the delivery of the Transition Services. The Seller Manager will coordinate and consult with the Company Manager (as defined in _Section 6(d)_) regarding the provision of the Transition Services. The Seller may, in its sole discretion, change the individual designated to serve as the Seller Manager upon at least ten (10) days prior written notice to the Company if feasible. (d) _Company Manager_. The Company will appoint an employee (the " _Company Manager_ ") to have overall responsibility for coordinating the receipt of the Transition Services. The Company Manager will coordinate and consult with the Seller Manager regarding the delivery of the Transition Services. The Company may, in its sole discretion, change the individual designated to serve as the Company Manager upon at least ten (10) days prior written notice to the Seller if feasible. 7. _Confidentiality_. Neither Party shall disclose or use any Confidential Information (defined below) of the other Party without the prior written consent of such other Party except as expressly permitted under this Agreement. Such restrictions do not extend to any item of information that (a) is or becomes publicly available without the fault of the receiving Party; (b) is disclosed or made available to the receiving Party by a third party without restriction and without breach of any relationship of confidentiality; or (c) is independently developed by the receiving Party without use of the disclosing Partys Confidential Information. It shall not be a breach of this Section 7 if Confidential Information is disclosed pursuant to subpoena or other compulsory judicial or administrative process, provided the Party served with such subpoena or process promptly notifies the other Party and provides reasonable assistance so that the other Party may seek a protective order against public disclosure. In addition, either Party shall have the right without having the obligation to obtain the prior consent of the other Party to disclose this Agreement or the existence of this Agreement if such Party is required to do so by the U.S. securities laws or the rules and regulations of the stock exchange upon which such Partys stock is listed. The obligations of confidentiality set forth in this Section 7 shall be in addition to, and shall not amend, modify or otherwise limit, any obligations of confidentiality or non-disclosure as set forth in the Purchase Agreement. For purposes of this Agreement, the term " _Confidential Information_ " means any information that may be disclosed or submitted by one Party to another Party that is marked or identified as confidential or which a reasonable person in the industry would consider to be confidential, including, without limitation, trade secrets, processes, techniques, drawings, designs, models, customer-related information and data, computer programs (in object code or source code), databases, business plans, technical data, product ideas, marketing data, contracts and financial information. 8. _IT Services_. If the Company uses any of the Sellers office equipment, telephones, computers or data processing, internet or communications services (whether or not identified in _Schedule A_ ), the Company shall adhere in all respects to the Sellers corporate information policies as in effect from time to time including, without limitation, policies with respect to protection of confidential information, data privacy and other policies regarding the use of such resources. 9. _No Warranty; Limitation of Liability; Indemnification_. (a) _No Warranty_. THE SELLER AND THE COMPANY EACH ACKNOWLEDGE AND AGREE THAT, EXCEPT AS PROVIDED IN _SECTION 2 (A)_, THE SELLER HAS AGREED TO PROVIDE THE TRANSITION SERVICES HEREUNDER AS AN ACCOMMODATION TO THE COMPANY AND THAT THE SELLER MAKES NO REPRESENTATIONS OR WARRANTIES WHATSOEVER, WHETHER EXPRESS OR IMPLIED BY STATUTE OR OTHERWISE, WITH RESPECT TO THE TRANSITION SERVICES OR ANY OTHER MATTERS RELATING TO OR ARISING OUT OF THIS AGREEMENT. (b) _Limitation of Liability_. NOTWITHSTANDING ANY OTHER PROVISION SET FORTH IN THIS AGREEMENT OR THE PURCHASE AGREEMENT TO THE CONTRARY, IN NO EVENT WILL THE SELLER, OR ITS SUBSIDIARIES, AFFILIATES OR SERVICE PROVIDERS, BE LIABLE FOR ANY SPECIAL, INCIDENTAL, INDIRECT, COLLATERAL, CONSEQUENTIAL OR PUNITIVE DAMAGES OR LOST PROFITS, HOWEVER CAUSED AND ON ANY THEORY OF LIABILITY, IN CONNECTION WITH ANY CLAIMS, LOSSES, DAMAGES OR INJURIES ARISING HEREUNDER, INCLUDING SCHEDULES OR EXHIBITS HERETO. IN NO EVENT WILL THE SELLERS TOTAL AGGREGATE LIABILITY UNDER THIS AGREEMENT EXCEED THE FEES RECEIVED BY THE SELLER UNDER THIS AGREEMENT FOR THE TRANSITION SERVICES. (c) _Seller Indemnification_. THE SELLER SHALL HAVE NO OBLIGATION UNDER THIS AGREEMENT TO INDEMNIFY THE COMPANY FOR INFRINGEMENT CLAIMS OR FOR ANY OTHER REASON WHATSOEVER. THE SELLERS OBLIGATION TO INDEMNIFY THE COMPANY, IF ANY, SHALL BE AS SET FORTH IN THE PURCHASE AGREEMENT AND SUBJECT TO THE TERMS, CONDITIONS AND LIMITATIONS SET FORTH THEREIN. 10. _Indemnity_. The Company agrees to indemnify, defend and hold harmless the Seller and each Service Provider and their respective employees, agents, officers and directors from and against any and all claims, demands, complaints, liabilities, losses, damages, costs and expenses (collectively, " _Damages_ ") arising from the negligent acts or omissions or willful misconduct of the Company or its Affiliates and their respective employees and agents in connection with the Transition Services. The Seller will provide prompt written notice to the Company of any such Damages and will provide the Company with reasonable cooperation in the defense thereof, at the Companys expense. 11. _Relationship of the Parties_. The Seller is and will remain at all times an independent contractor of the Company in the performance of the Transition Services. In all matters relating to this Agreement, each Party will be solely responsible for the acts of its employees and agents, and employees or agents of one Party shall not be considered employees or agents of the other Party. Except as otherwise provided herein, no Party will have any right, power or authority to create any obligation, express or implied, on behalf of any other Party nor shall either Party act or represent or hold itself out as having authority to act as an agent or partner of the other Party, or in any way bind or commit the other Party to any obligations. Nothing in this Agreement is intended to create or constitute a joint venture, partnership, agency, trust or other association of any kind between the Parties or persons referred to herein and each Party shall be responsible only for its respective obligations as set forth in this Agreement. 12. _Compliance with Laws_. Each Party will comply with all applicable laws, rules, ordinances and regulations of any governmental entity or regulatory agency governing the Transition Services. No Party will take any action in violation of any applicable law, rule, ordinance or regulation that could reasonably be expected to result in liability being imposed on the other Party. 13. _Binding Effect and Assignment_. This Agreement binds and benefits the Parties and their respective permitted successors and assigns. The Company may not assign any of its rights or delegate any of its obligations under this Agreement without the written consent of the Seller, which consent may be withheld in the Sellers sole and absolute discretion and any assignment or attempted assignment in violation of the foregoing shall be null and void. The Seller may delegate its duties to provide the Transition Services hereunder in the manner permitted under Section 1, Section 6(a) and Section 6(c) of this Agreement. 14. _Entire Agreement; Amendments_. This Agreement and the Purchase Agreement (and the agreements and other documents referred to herein and therein) constitute the final agreement between the Parties with respect to the subject matter hereof and thereof, and are the complete and exclusive statement of the Parties agreement on the matters contained herein and therein. All prior and contemporaneous negotiations and agreements between the Parties with respect to the matters contained herein are superseded by this Agreement. The Parties may amend this Agreement only by a written agreement signed by both Parties that identifies itself as an amendment to this Agreement. 15. _Force Majeure_. In the event that the Seller or any Service Provider is delayed in, or prevented from, performing its obligations under this Agreement, in whole or in part, due to an act of God, fire, flood, storm, explosion, civil disorder, strike, lockout or other labor trouble, material shortages of utilities, facilities, labor, materials or equipment, delay in transportation, breakdown or accident, any law, order, proclamation, regulation, ordinance, demand or requirement of any governmental authority, riot, war, acts of terror, rebellion, or other cause beyond the reasonable control of the Seller or the applicable Service Provider (each a " _Force Majeure Event_ "), then (a) the affected provisions and/or other requirements of this Agreement shall be suspended to the extent necessary during the period of such disability, and (b) the Seller shall have no liability to the Company or any other party in connection therewith. The Seller shall resume full performance of this Agreement as soon as reasonably practicable following the conclusion of the Force Majeure Event. 16. _Severability_. If any provision of this Agreement is determined to be invalid, illegal or unenforceable, the remaining provisions of this Agreement shall remain in full force, if the essential terms and conditions of this Agreement for each Party remain valid, binding and enforceable. 17. _Counterparts_. The Parties may execute this Agreement in multiple counterparts, each of which constitutes an original of the Party that signed it, and all of which together constitute one agreement. The signatures of both Parties need not appear on the same counterpart. The delivery of signed counterparts by facsimile or email transmission that includes a copy of the sending Partys signature is as effective as signing and delivering the counterpart in person. 18. _Notices_. This Agreement shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the domestic laws of the State of Delaware without giving effect to any choice or conflict of law provision or rule (whether of the State of Delaware or any other jurisdiction) that would cause the application of the laws of any jurisdiction other than the State of Delaware. 21. _Jurisdiction; Waiver of Jury Trial_.
